             <script type="text/javascript">
              to_ajax_show_shoppingcar_watermark();
                                                                                                 var timeout = 0;
                                                 function dropBasket() {
 
 //                                                    $('html, body').scrollTop(0);
                                                     var obj_x = $('#test').offset().top;
                                                     var obj_y = $('#test').offset().left - ( 300 -$('#test').width() );
                                                     var bagCarHeight = 200;
                                                     var scorllHeight = get_bag_height();
                                                     var windowHeight = $(window).height();
                                                     var windowThreeFifths = windowHeight / 5 * 3;
 
                                                     if($(window).height() > obj_x){
                                                         if(scorllHeight > windowThreeFifths){
                                                             bagCarHeight = windowHeight - obj_x - 120;
                                                             $("#inlineBagCar_content").css("padding-right" , "0px");
                                                         }else{
                                                             bagCarHeight = scorllHeight + 20;
                                                             $("#inlineBagCar_content_outlayer").css("overflow" , "hidden");
                                                         }
                                                     }
                                                     $("#inlineBagCar_content").css("height", (bagCarHeight + "px"));
 
                                                     $('#inlineBagCar_content').on( 'mousewheel', function ( e ) {
                                                         var event = e.originalEvent,
                                                             d = event.wheelDelta || -event.detail;
                                                             this.scrollTop += ( d < 0 ? 1 : -1 ) * 30;
                                                             e.preventDefault();
                                                     });
                                                     $("#inlineBagCar").css("top", (obj_x + $('#test').height()) + "px");
                                                     $("#inlineBagCar").css("left", obj_y + "px");
                                                     $("#inlineBagCar").show();
                                                     $("#inlineBagCar_footer").show();
                                                     $("#inlineBagCar_content").stop().slideDown("slow", function () {
                                                          timeout = setTimeout("close_basket_slider()", 4000);
                                                         $("#inlineBagCar").hover(function () {
                                                             window.clearTimeout(timeout);
                                                         },function(){
                                                              timeout = setTimeout("close_basket_slider()", 4000);
                                                         });
                                                     });
                                                 }
                                                 function close_basket_slider() {
                                                     $("#inlineBagCar_content").stop().slideUp("slow", function () {
                                                         $("#inlineBagCar").hide();
                                                         $("#inlineBagCar_footer").hide();
                                                     });
                                                 }
 
                                                 function get_bag_height(){
                                                     $("#inlineBagCar").css("visibility","hidden").show();
                                                     $("#inlineBagCar_footer").css("visibility","hidden").show();
                                                     $("#inlineBagCar_content").css("visibility","hidden").show();
                                                     var contentHeight = $("#inlineBagCar_content_outlayer").height();
                                                     $("#inlineBagCar").css("visibility","visible").hide();
                                                     $("#inlineBagCar_footer").css("visibility","visible").hide();
                                                     $("#inlineBagCar_content").css("visibility","visible").hide();
                                                     return contentHeight;
                                                 }
             </script>

       <script type="text/javascript">
        //ie slideup flashing fix -- start
 (function(){
 	// Define overriding method.
 	jQuery.fx.prototype.hide = function(){
 	this.options.orig[this.prop] = jQuery.style(this.elem,this.prop);
 	this.options.hide = true;
 	this.custom(this.cur(),1);
 	}
 })();
 //ie slideup flashing fix -- end
 
 $(document).ready(function(){
     var isTouch = false;
     $('td.menu_item_td').on('touchstart', function(e) {
         $this = $(this);
         if(isTouch) {
             $this.trigger('mouseleave');
         } else {
             $this.trigger('mouseenter');
         }
     });
 
 	$('td.menu_item_td').hoverIntent({
 		sensitivity: 9,
 		interval: 50,
 		timeout: 700,
 		over: function(){
 			$this = $(this);
 			current_pos = $this.index();
 			_pos = ($('table.topA_3_middle_data_table tr').children('td').length)/2;
 			_align = (current_pos >= _pos)?'right':'left';
 			pos_x = (current_pos >= _pos)?'0':'0';
             isTouch = true;
             var target = $this.children('div').children('div.dropmenudiv_E');
             var windowWidth = $( window ).width();
             target.css({ position: "absolute", visibility: "hidden", display: "block" });
             var targetWidth = target.width();
             var offsetLeft = target.offset().left;
             target.css({ position: "", visibility: "", display: "" });
             offsetLeft = offsetLeft + targetWidth;
             if(offsetLeft > windowWidth){
                 var newOffset = windowWidth - targetWidth - 20;
                 target.css('top',0).css(_align,pos_x).slideDown().offset({left:newOffset}).attr("data-left", _align);
             }else{
                 target.css('top',0).css(_align,pos_x).slideDown();
             }
 		},
 		out: function(){
 			$this = $(this);
 			var targetOut = $this.children('div').children('div.dropmenudiv_E');
             var attr = targetOut.attr("data-left");
             if (attr && attr !== false) {
                 targetOut.slideUp().removeAttr("data-left").css(attr,"0px");
             }else{
                 targetOut.slideUp();
             }
             isTouch = false;
 		}
 	});
                 });
       </script>

     <script>
      $(function () {
         $("#pagenation_ad_full_top .thumbs_list>li").hover(function () {
             $(".content_title", this).show();
             $(".content_title_text", this).show();
             var id = $(this).attr("id") + "_pic";
             $(this).parents(".photo_box2,.photo_box3,.photo_box4").children(".main_box").children(".main_box_list").children("li").each(function (idx) {
                 if ($(this).attr("id") !== id) {
                     $(this).stop(true, true).fadeOut(450);
                 }
             });
             $("#" + id).stop(true, true).fadeIn(450
                             );
         }, function () {
             $(".content_title", this).hide();
             $(".content_title_text", this).hide();
         });
     });
     </script>

     <script src="//fs1.shop123.com.tw/images_pro/share_utf8/js/hammer.min.js" type="text/javascript">
     </script>
     <script type="text/javascript">
      var interval;
         var timer = function () {
             clearInterval(timer);
             interval = window.setInterval(function () {
                 var $elm = $("#full_top_mq3_ul .mq3_li_on");
                 var index = $elm.closest("li").index();
                 index = index + 1;
                 if (index >= $("#full_top_mq3_ul li").length) {
                     index = 0;
                 }
                 var $obj = $('ul#full_top_mq3_ul li:eq(' + (index) + ')').find("img.slide-img-short");
                 hoverEventLike($obj);
             }, 5000);
         };
 
         var imageList = {};
 
         function hoverEventLike($obj) {
             var $hyperA = $obj.closest("li").find(".full_top_ad3").clone();
             var newSrc = $obj.attr("data-bigimg");
             var arror_target = $obj.closest("li").find(".li_arrow_class");
             $("ul#full_top_mq3_ul li").addClass("mq3_li_off").removeClass("mq3_li_on");
             $obj.closest("li").addClass("mq3_li_on").removeClass("mq3_li_off");
             $hyperA.append(imageList[newSrc]);
             $(".slide-img-short-hyper").replaceWith($hyperA.addClass('slide-img-short-hyper'));
             $("ul#full_top_mq3_ul .li_arrow_class").css('visibility', 'hidden');
             arror_target.css('visibility', 'visible');
         }
 
         $('document').ready(function () { // init
             $('.slide-img-short').each(function (e, v) {
                 var image = document.createElement("IMG");
                 image.src = $(v).data("bigimg");
                 imageList[$(v).data("bigimg")] = image;
             });
 
             hoverEventLike($("ul#full_top_mq3_ul li:eq(0)").find(".slide-img-short"));
             $("ul#full_top_mq3_ul li").hover(
                 function () {
                     window.clearInterval(interval);
                     var $obj = $(this).find("img.slide-img-short");
                     hoverEventLike($obj);
                 },
                 function () {
                     timer();
                 }
             );
             timer();
             try {
                 new Hammer($("#full_top_mq3_div_temp")[0], {
                     domEvents: true
                 });
 
                 $("#full_top_mq3_div_temp").on("swipeleft", function (e) {
                     var obj = $(".mod-ad-fulltop-page .mq3_li_on").next();
                     if (obj.length == 0) {
                         obj = $("#full_top_mq3_ul li").first()
                     }
                     var imageShort = obj.find("img.slide-img-short");
                     hoverEventLike(imageShort);
                 }).on("swiperight", function (e) {
                     var obj = $(".mod-ad-fulltop-page .mq3_li_on").prev();
                     if (obj.length == 0) {
                         obj = $("#full_top_mq3_ul li").last()
                     }
                     var imageShort = obj.find("img.slide-img-short");
                     hoverEventLike(imageShort);
                 });
             } catch (e) {
                 console.log(e);
             }
 
         });
     </script>

     <script type="text/javascript">
      function banner_popup_top(sn, target) {
         $.ajax({
             url: "ajax_website_module_api.php?module_type=ajax_get_banner_popup&banner_sn=" + sn,
             type: "GET",
             dataType: "text",
             success: function (response) {
 
                 $("#banner_popup").html("<div style='position:absolute;right: 0px;top: 0px ;'><a href='javascript:close_popup();'><img src='//fs1.shop123.com.tw/images_pro/300120/space.gif' title='banner_popup_close_icon' class='display_off'></a></div>" + response);
                 setTimeout(function () {
                     show_popup_top(target);
                 }, 0);
 
             }
         });
 
     }
     function show_popup_top(target) {
 
         var banner_width = $("#banner_popup").width();
         var banner_height = $("#banner_popup").height() / 2;
         var left = target.offset().left + target.width() / 2 - banner_width / 2;
         $.blockUI({
             message: $('#banner_popup'),
             overlayCSS: {
                 backgroundColor: '#000',
                 opacity: 0.5,
                 cursor: 'auto'
             },
             css: {
                 border: '0px',
                 top: '50%',
                 left: left + 'px',
                 textAlign: 'left',
                 width: banner_width + 'px',
                 marginTop: "-" + banner_height + "px",
                 background: '#FFF',
                 cursor: 'auto'
 
             }
         });
         $('.blockOverlay').attr('title', '單擊關閉').click(function () {
             close_popup();
         });
 
                 setTimeout("close_popup()",3000);
             }
     function close_popup() {
         $('#banner_popup').slideUp(1000, $.unblockUI);
     }
     </script>

       <script language="javascript">
        function to_clear2(){
 	with(document.frmSearch1){
 		keyword.value = "";
 	}
 }
 function to_return2(){
 	with(document.frmSearch1){
 		if(keyword.value == "") keyword.value = "關鍵字";
 	}
 }
 function to_clear3(){
 	with(document.frmSearch1){
 		keyword_id.value = "";
 	}
 }
 function to_return3(){
 	with(document.frmSearch1){
 		if(keyword_id.value == "") keyword_id.value = "請輸入產品序號";
 	}
 }
       </script>

          <script type="text/javascript">
           function banner_popup(sn, target) {
 
             $.ajax({
                 url: "ajax_website_module_api.php?module_type=ajax_get_banner_popup&banner_sn=" + sn,
                 type: "GET",
                 dataType: "text",
                 success: function (response) {
                     $("#banner_popup").html("<div style='position:absolute;right: 0px;top: 0px ;'><a href='javascript:close_popup();'><img src='//fs1.shop123.com.tw/images_pro/300120/space.gif' title='banner_popup_close_icon' class='display_off'></a></div>" + response);
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         show_popup(target);
                     }, 0);
                 }
             });
 
         }
         function show_popup(target) {
 
 
             var banner_width = $("#banner_popup").width();
             var banner_height = $("#banner_popup").height() / 2;
             var left = target.offset().left + target.width() / 2 - banner_width / 2;
             $.blockUI({
                 message: $('#banner_popup'),
                 overlayCSS: {
                     backgroundColor: '#000',
                     opacity: 0.5,
                     cursor: 'auto'
                 },
                 css: {
                     border: '0px',
                     top: '50%',
                     left: left + 'px',
                     textAlign: 'left',
                     width: banner_width + 'px',
                     marginTop: "-" + banner_height + "px",
                     background: '#FFF',
                     cursor: 'auto'
 
                 }
             });
             $('.blockOverlay').attr('title', '單擊關閉').click(function () {
                 close_popup();
             });
                         setTimeout("close_popup()",3000);
                     }
         function close_popup() {
             $('#banner_popup').slideUp(1000, $.unblockUI);
         }
          </script>

          </script>
          <script type="text/javascript">
           (function (win, $) {
             var middleTopAdBBlock = {
                 mid_top_b_t: null,
                 mid_top_b_change_ad_img: function (ad_sn) {
                     if ($('.mod-ad-min-page div#mid_top_b_mq3_div a').length > 1) {
                         var obj_a = '#mid_top_b_ad3_a_' + ad_sn;
                         var obj_li = '#mid_top_b_ad3_li_' + ad_sn;
                         var obj_img = '#mid_top_b_ad3_li_' + ad_sn + ' img#li_arrow';
 
                         // banner 圖片
                         $('.mod-ad-min-page div#mid_top_b_mq3_div a:not(' + obj_a + ')').hide();
                         $(obj_a).show();
 
                         // 頁籤標題
                         $('.mod-ad-min-page ul#mid_top_b_mq3_ul li').removeClass('mq3_li_on').removeClass('mq3_li_off');
                         $('.mod-ad-min-page ul#mid_top_b_mq3_ul li:not(' + obj_li + ')').addClass('mq3_li_off');
                         $(obj_li).addClass('mq3_li_on');
 
                         // 頁籤圖片
                         $('.mod-ad-min-page ul#mid_top_b_mq3_ul li img#li_arrow').css('visibility', 'hidden');
                         $(obj_img).css('visibility', 'visible');
                     }
                 },
                 mid_top_b_mq3_timer: function () { //輪播
                     var ad_sn = arguments[0];
                     this.mid_top_b_change_ad_img(ad_sn);
                     ad_sn++;
                     var ad3_amount = 3;
                     if (ad_sn > ad3_amount) {
                         ad_sn = 1;
                     }
                     this.mid_top_b_t = setTimeout("mid_top_b_mq3_timer(" + ad_sn + ")", 5000);
                 },
                 mid_top_b_get_curr_ad_sn: function (e) {
                     var begin = e.target.id.length - 1;
                     var curr_ad_sn = e.target.id.substr(begin, 1);
                     return curr_ad_sn;
                 }
             };
 
             win.middleTopAdBBlock = middleTopAdBBlock;
 
             var require = function () {
                 var url = arguments[0];
                 var callback = arguments[1];
 
                 $.ajaxSetup({
                     cache: true
                 });
 
                 $.ajax({
                     url: url,
                     dataType: "script",
                     success: function () {
                         callback();
                     }
                 })
 
             };
 
             win.require = require;
 
         })(window, jQuery);
 
         require("//fs1.shop123.com.tw/images_pro/share_utf8/js/jquery.hoverIntent.js", function () {
             $('.mod-ad-min-page ul#mid_top_b_mq3_ul li').hoverIntent(
                 function (e) {
                     var curr_ad_sn = middleTopAdBBlock.mid_top_b_get_curr_ad_sn(e);
                     if (curr_ad_sn) {
                         clearTimeout(middleTopAdBBlock.mid_top_b_t);
                         middleTopAdBBlock.mid_top_b_change_ad_img(curr_ad_sn);
                     }
                 },
                 function (e) {
                     var curr_ad_sn = middleTopAdBBlock.mid_top_b_get_curr_ad_sn(e);
                     if (curr_ad_sn) {
                         middleTopAdBBlock.mid_top_b_mq3_timer(curr_ad_sn);
                     }
                 }
             );
 
             $('.mod-ad-min-page ul#mid_top_b_mq3_ul li:first-child').removeClass('mq3_li_off').addClass('mq3_li_on');
             $('.mod-ad-min-page ul#mid_top_b_mq3_ul li:first-child img').css('visibility', 'visible');
             middleTopAdBBlock.mid_top_b_mq3_timer(1);
         });
          </script>

       <script>
        $(function(){
     $("#pagenation_e_ad_middle_down .thumbs_list>li").hover(function(){
         $(".content_title",this).show();
         $(".content_title_text",this).show();
         var id = $(this).attr("id")+"_pic";
         $(this).parents(".photo_box2,.photo_box3,.photo_box4").children(".main_box").children(".main_box_list").children("li").each(function(idx){
             if($(this).attr("id") !== id){
                 $(this).stop(true,true).fadeOut(450);
             }
         });
         $("#"+id).stop(true,true).fadeIn(450);
     },function(){
         $(".content_title",this).hide();
         $(".content_title_text",this).hide();
     });
 });
       </script>

                     banner.start();
                 });

              <script>
               $(function () {
         $("body").on("click", ".product_box_size", function () {
             $(this).parent().children(".product_box_size_unselected,.product_box_size_selected").each(function () {
                 $(this).removeClass("product_box_size_unselected").removeClass("product_box_size_selected").addClass("product_box_size_unselected");
             });
             $(this).removeClass("product_box_size_unselected").removeClass("product_box_size_selected").addClass("product_box_size_selected");
             var value = $(this).attr("data-value");
             var car_sn = $(this).attr("data-carsn");
             $("#product_list_car_sn_" + car_sn).attr("value", value);
             to_change_product_color_item_price(document.getElementById("product_list_car_sn_" + car_sn), car_sn);
         });
     });
              </script>

     <script type="text/javascript">
      $(function(){
         $("#pagenation_ad_full_down .thumbs_list>li").hover(function(){
             $(".content_title",this).show();
             $(".content_title_text",this).show();
             var id = $(this).attr("id")+"_pic";
             $(this).parents(".photo_box2,.photo_box3,.photo_box4").children(".main_box").children(".main_box_list").children("li").each(function(idx){
                 if($(this).attr("id") !== id){
                     $(this).stop(true,true).fadeOut(450);
                 }
             });
             $("#" + id).stop(true, true).fadeIn(450
                             );
         },function(){
             $(".content_title",this).hide();
             $(".content_title_text",this).hide();
         });
     });
 
     function banner_popup(sn,target) {
 
         $.ajax({
             url:"ajax_website_module_api.php?module_type=ajax_get_banner_popup&banner_sn="+sn,
             type : "GET",
             dataType:"text",
             success : function(response){
                 $("#banner_popup").html(response);
                 setTimeout(function(){show_popup(target);},0);
             }
         });
 
     }
 
     function show_popup(target){
 
         var banner_width = $("#banner_popup").width();
         var banner_height = $("#banner_popup").height()/2;
         var left = target.offset().left + target.width()/2 - banner_width/2;
         $.blockUI({
             message: $('#banner_popup'),
             overlayCSS: {
                 backgroundColor: '#000',
                 opacity: 0.5,
                 cursor: 'auto'
             },
             css: {
                 border: '0px',
                 top: '50%',
                 left: left+'px',
                 textAlign: 'left',
                 width: banner_width+'px',
                 marginTop: "-"+banner_height+"px",
                 background: '#FFF',
                 cursor: 'auto'
 
             }
         });
         $( '.blockOverlay' ).attr( 'title' , '單擊關閉' ).click(function(){
             close_popup();
         });
         setTimeout("close_popup()",3000);
     }
     function close_popup(){
         $('#banner_popup').slideUp(1000,$.unblockUI);
     }
     //輪播式
     $(function(){
         var banner = $("#ad_full_down_banner").banner({
             effect:"fadeIn",
             speed:5000,
             list_btn:true,
             responsive: false        });
         $("#ad_full_down_slider").mouseover(function(){
             banner.stop();
         });
         $("#ad_full_down_slider").mouseout(function(){
             banner.start();
         });
     });
     //頁簽式
     function mid_top_b_change_ad_img(ad_sn){
         if($('.mod-ad-fullbtm-page div#mid_top_b_mq3_div a').length > 1 ){
             var obj_a = '#mid_top_b_ad3_a_'+ad_sn;
             var obj_li = '#mid_top_b_ad3_li_'+ad_sn;
             var obj_img = '#mid_top_b_ad3_li_'+ad_sn+' img#li_arrow';
             // banner 圖片
             $('div#mid_top_b_mq3_div a:not('+obj_a+')').hide();
             $(obj_a).show();
 
             // 頁籤標題
             $('.mod-ad-fullbtm-page ul#mid_top_b_mq3_ul li').removeClass('mq3_li_on').removeClass('mq3_li_off');
             $('.mod-ad-fullbtm-page ul#mid_top_b_mq3_ul li:not('+obj_li+')').addClass('mq3_li_off');
             $(obj_li).addClass('mq3_li_on');
 
             // 頁籤圖片
             $('.mod-ad-fullbtm-page ul#mid_top_b_mq3_ul li img#li_arrow').css('visibility','hidden');
             $(obj_img).css('visibility','visible');
         }
     }
 
     function mid_top_b_mq3_timer(ad_sn){ //輪播
         mid_top_b_change_ad_img(ad_sn);
         ad_sn++;
         var ad3_amount = $(".mod-ad-fullbtm-page #mid_top_b_mq3_div a").length;
         if(ad_sn > ad3_amount){ad_sn = 1;}
         mid_top_b_t = setTimeout("mid_top_b_mq3_timer("+ad_sn+")",5000);
     }
 
     function mid_top_b_get_curr_ad_sn(e){
         var begin = e.target.id.length-1;
         var curr_ad_sn = e.target.id.substr(begin,1);
         return curr_ad_sn;
     }
 
     $('document').ready(function(){ // init
         $('.mod-ad-fullbtm-page ul#mid_top_b_mq3_ul li').hoverIntent(
             function(e){
                 var curr_ad_sn = mid_top_b_get_curr_ad_sn(e);
                 if(curr_ad_sn){
                     clearTimeout(mid_top_b_t);
                     mid_top_b_change_ad_img(curr_ad_sn);
                 }
             },
             function(e){
                 var curr_ad_sn = mid_top_b_get_curr_ad_sn(e);
                 if(curr_ad_sn){
                     mid_top_b_mq3_timer(curr_ad_sn);
                 }
             }
         );
 
         $('.mod-ad-fullbtm-page ul#mid_top_b_mq3_ul li:first-child').removeClass('mq3_li_off').addClass('mq3_li_on');
         $('.mod-ad-fullbtm-page ul#mid_top_b_mq3_ul li:first-child img').css('visibility','visible');
         mid_top_b_mq3_timer(1);
     });
     </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(window).load(function(){
             var _titleHeight = 0;
 
             $('.abgne_tip_gallery_block').each(function(index, v){
                     var $this = $(this);
                     var $caption = $('.caption', $this),
                         _speed = 500;
                     var img_width;
                     var img_height;
                     var box_height=$('.caption').eq(0).height();
                     $this.hover(function(){
                         img_height = $('img', $this).height();
                         img_width = $('img', $this).width();
                         $caption.css("top",img_height  + 5+"px");
                         $caption.css("width",(img_width-60)+"px");
                         $caption.stop().animate({
                             top: img_height - box_height  + 5
                         }, _speed);
                     }, function(){
                         img_height = $('img', $this).height();
                         img_width = $('img', $this).width();
                         $caption.css("top",img_height + 5 +"px");
                         $caption.css("width",(img_width-60)+"px");
                         $caption.stop().animate({
                             top: img_height + 5
                         }, _speed);
                     });
             });
     });
 
     /**
      * 解決 a link 中 同時有 onmouseOver 的 event 把 herf replace 為 #;
      * 因為在手機版中 並沒有 onmouseover的狀態，如果同時有a link 又有 mouseover的狀態
      * 將會導致 onmouseover無法正常呈現．
      * 所以判斷 1手機 2.a link 中 有 onmouseover 就進行替換
      */
 
     $(document).ready(function () {
         //$_SESSION["user_agent_device"] = $user_agent_device; From novel.php
         var userAgentDevice = '0';
         if (userAgentDevice == 1) {
             $("a").each(function (i, v) {
                 var mouseoverEvent = new String($(v).attr("onmouseover"));
                 var dataDropit = $(v).data("dropit");
                 if (!mouseoverEvent.indexOf("cssdropdown.dropit(this,event,")) {
                     $(v).attr("href", "#");
                 }else if(dataDropit!==undefined&&dataDropit===true){
                     $(v).attr("href", "#");
                 }
             });
         }
     });
   </script>
